     # The fix slightly changes HTMLParser's output, so tests for\n   122→        # particularly malformed input must handle both old and new results.\n   123→        # The check below is temporary until all supported Python versions and\n   124→        # CI workers include the fix. See:\n   125→        # https://github.com/python/cpython/commit/6eb6c5db\n   126→        min_fixed_security = {\n   127→            (3, 13): (3, 13, 6),\n   128→            (3, 12): (3, 12, 12),\n   129→        }\n   130→        # Similarly, there was a fix for terminating incomplete entities. See:\n   131→        # https://github.com/python/cpython/commit/95296a9d\n   132→        min_fixed_incomplete_entities = {\n   133→            (3, 14): (3, 14, 1),\n   134→            (3, 13): (3, 13, 10),\n   135→            (3, 12): (3, 12, math.inf),  # not fixed in 3.12.\n   136→        }\n   137→        major_version = sys.version_info[:2]\n   138→        htmlparser_fixed_security = sys.version_info >= min_fixed_security.get(\n   139→            major_version, major_version\n   140→        )\n   141→        htmlparser_fixed_incomplete_entities = (\n   142→            sys.version_info\n   143→            >= min_fixed_incomplete_entities.get(major_version, major_version)\n   144→        )\n   145→        items = (\n   146→            (\n   147→          (\"<x>b<y>\", \"b\"),\n   163→            (\"a<p onclick=\\\"alert('<test>')\\\">b</p>c\", \"abc\"),\n   164→            (\"a<p a >b</p>c\", \"abc\"),\n   165→            (\"d<a:b           # https://bugs.python.org/issue20288\n   169→            (\"&gotcha&#;<>\", \"&gotcha&#;<>\"),\n   170→            (\"<sc<!-- -->ript>test<<!-- -->/script>\", \"ript>test\"),\n   171→            (\n   172→                \"<script>alert()</script>&h\",\n   173→                \"alert()&h;\" if htmlparser_fixed_incomplete_entities else \"alert()h\",\n   174→            ),\n   175→
